         R3: (0, 10) -> (0, 7)   (bridge down from R3_t to R2_s)
         R2: (0, 6) -> (5, 4)   (bridge down from R2_t to R1_s)
         R1: (5, 3) -> (1, 0)
     10. whole: s=(0, 10) -> t=(3, 0)
         R3: (0, 10) -> (0, 7)   (bridge down from R3_t to R2_s)
         R2: (0, 6) -> (5, 4)   (bridge down from R2_t to R1_s)
         R1: (5, 3) -> (3, 0)
